# Error Analysis and Resolution

## Error 1: `log.subsetMesh` — Cannot find file `constant/polyMesh/sets/c0`

This error occurs because the `topoSet` command was run to create cell sets for the obstacle, but the `subsetMesh` command is trying to read a set file (`c0`) that doesn't exist. The `topoSet` command creates multiple set files (`c0`, `c1`, `c2`, ..., `c10`) corresponding to each `boxToCell` action in the `topoSetDict`. However, the `subsetMesh` command is likely being called with a subset specification that references `c0`, which may not have been created or may have been renamed.

**Resolution:**
- After running `topoSet`, verify that the set files were created. The `topoSetDict` contains 11 actions, so you should see `c0` through `c10`. If `c0` is missing, check the `topoSetDict` — the first action creates `c0` via `new`, and subsequent actions use `add` which appends to existing sets. The issue may be that `subsetMesh` is being called incorrectly or the set names don't match what `subsetMesh` expects.
- Alternatively, if `subsetMesh` is being called with a subset specification that doesn't correspond to any of the created sets, adjust the `subsetMesh` command to use the correct set name (e.g., `c1` through `c10` or use a different subset specification entirely).
- If the goal is to remove the obstacle cells from the mesh, consider using `subsetMesh` with a negative set name (e.g., `subsetMesh -overwrite -patch walls -patch atmosphere -patch defaultFaces
